Hi Adhamh

Creating a bugzilla account didn't work, so I thought I could have a look at
the nib file and try, did my first editing of a nib file since I used
rhapsody... (I just touched it then) 

I'm sending you the corrected nib, there were two Convert buttons, both
catching Return and the one that won didn't have the binding, and was
pulsating behind the inactive one...

Best,

Stefan
